layout: "post"
title: "The circle"
date: "2018-05-01"
agda: true
toc: true
categories: type-theory
---

In this entry, we want to show some equivalences
between the circle and other higher inductive types.

{% comment %}

{: . equation }

  $$\sum\,{\mathbb{S}^1}\,(\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbb{S}^1}\, \mathcal{U}\,  2\,
  (\mathsf{ua}(\mathsf{rec}_{2}2 1_{2} 0_{2}))) \simeq \mathbb{S}^1.$$

I gave a talk giving one solution using the flattening lemma:

- [**Direct link PDF**](https://github.com/jonaprieto/flattenlem/files/2045561/Jonathan-Prieto-Cubides-The-Flattening-Lemma.pdf)

{% endcomment %}

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="616" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="621" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="628" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">2018-07-06-mini-hott</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

##  S¹ type

The circle is the higher inductive type with one point
and one no trivial path called path as we show in the following
picture.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/circle.png)
*Figure 1. The circle type `S¹`.*

## `pS` type

![path](/assets/ipe-images/tour-type.png)
*Figure 2. `pS` Type.*

## Equivalences

### Lemma 1

{: .equation }

  $$ \mathsf{S}^{1} \simeq \mathsf{pS}. $$

**Proof**.

Let us define the outgoing functions:

The proof of the homotopy $$ f' ∘ g' \sim \mathsf{id}$$.

          <a id="8388" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#5179" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="8393" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#2058" class="Function">pS₀</a>
        <a id="8405" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7833" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof of the homotopy $$g' ∘ f' \sim \mathsf{id}$$:

- Action on paths of pairs

### Lemma 3

{: .equation}
  $$
    \Sigma~S^{1}~P~\simeq~pS
  $$

  where $$P (\mathsf{base}) :≡ \mathsf{Bool}$$ and $$\mathsf{ap~P~loop~=~ua~(neg)}$$.

<a id="Pbase=Bool"></a><a id="11952" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#11952" class="Function">Pbase=Bool</a> <a id="11963" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11965" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#11902" class="Function">P</a> <a id="11967" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#961" class="Function">base</a> <a id="11972" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#5044" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="11975" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3036" class="Datatype">Bool</a>
<a id="11980" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#11952" class="Function">Pbase=Bool</a> <a id="11991" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11993" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#5098" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>

<a id="11998" class="Comment">-- Pbase=Bool-family= : (λ z → P z) == (λ _ → Bool)</a>
<a id="12050" class="Comment">-- Pbase=Bool-family= rewrite Pbase=Bool = funext (S¹-ind (λ b → P b == Bool ) Pbase=Bool dpath)</a>
<a id="12147" class="Comment">--   where</a>
<a id="12158" class="Comment">--     dpath :  Pbase=Bool == Pbase=Bool [ (λ b → P b == Bool) ↓ loop ]</a>
<a id="12230" class="Comment">--     dpath =</a>
<a id="12245" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="12260" class="Comment">--         transport (λ b → P b == Bool) loop Pbase=Bool</a>
<a id="12317" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ transport-eq-fun-l P loop Pbase=Bool ⟩</a>
<a id="12373" class="Comment">--         ! ap P loop · Pbase=Bool</a>
<a id="12409" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! r · Pbase=Bool) (S¹-βrec Type₀ Bool (ua (neg-eq))) ⟩</a>
<a id="12491" class="Comment">--         ! ua (neg-eq) · Pbase=Bool</a>
<a id="12529" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! r · Pbase=Bool) {! !} ⟩</a>
<a id="12582" class="Comment">--         ! {! !} · Pbase=Bool</a>
<a id="12614" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ {! !} ⟩</a>
<a id="12639" class="Comment">--         Pbase=Bool</a>
<a id="12661" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>

<a id="12673" class="Comment">-- aux : transport (λ z → P z) loop == transport (λ _ → Bool) loop</a>
